### Important Data Source Note
> **Notice:** SYNTHETIC - linear interpolation between hourly measured points. Sub-hour values are NOT measured.

## 2. Executive Process Analysis

During this 6-hour period of **Startup Operation**, the Urea plant transition and ramping characteristics are clearly visible:
- **Urea Production Load (`UREA-LOAD`):** Started at **0.0%** and was successfully ramped up to a near-normal operation load of **97.0%** by the end of the 6-hour window, averaging **73.53%** over the startup period.
- **Pressure & Speed Ramping:** Synthesis pressure (`PT-329201`) ramped from an initial low of **3.3 bar** up to **139.6 bar** as the process pressurized. Concurrently, compressor/pump speed (`SIC-321951`) ramped from a stationary **-0.2%** (representing idle/stop) up to **126.8%** at peak startup feed rates.
- **Temperature Ramping:** Reactor temperatures demonstrate massive thermal transient behavior. For instance, the reactor bed transmitter `TT-322013` ramped from a cold/warm state of **152.1°C** up to **186.9°C** as the exothermic urea synthesis reaction became fully established.
- **Level & Control Valves:** Level transmitter `LT-322504-3` and associated level valves (`LV-322501`) show dynamic control changes as liquid levels in separator units were established, starting from 0.03% and peaking at 99.94% during startup surges, stabilized towards standard operating levels later.

## 3. Process Tag Dictionary

Below is an overview of the key process instrument tags represented in this dataset, grouped by measurement type:

| Tag Name | Measurement Category | Description |
|---|---|---|
| `UREA-LOAD` | Production Load | Plant production load indicator, in % of design capacity |
| `SIC-321951` | Speed Indicator/Controller | Machine speed controller (e.g., CO2 compressor turbine or Ammonia feed pump driver) |
| `FY-322403`, `FYM-322403` | Flow Control / Measurement | Raw material feed flows (Liquid NH3 or gaseous CO2) to synthesis section |
| `PT-329201`, `PT-329206`, `PT-321202` | Pressure Transmitter | High-pressure synthesis reactor loop, CO2 feed, or separator pressures |
| `PIC-329204`, `PIC-322203` | Pressure Indicator Controller | Controller loop setpoints/values for loop backpressure or downstream separators |
| `PV-322203` | Pressure Control Valve | Pressure control valve position/output corresponding to PIC-322203 |
| `TT-322002` to `TT-322017`, `TT-321001` | Temperature Transmitter | Synthesis reactor bed thermal sensors, preheater, stripper, or condenser temperatures |
| `TIC-329005` | Temperature Indicator Controller | Thermal loop controller, e.g., synthesis reactor top/bottom or condenser steam jacket |
| `TDY-329125` | Temperature Differential | Differential temperature calculation across critical heat exchangers or reactor beds |
| `LIC-322501`, `LV-322501` | Level Indicator Controller / Valve | High-pressure separator/scrubber level controller and associated discharge control valve |
| `HIC-322604`, `HIC-322605` | Hand Indicator Controller | Manual or hand-regulated control valves for feed adjustment or gas venting |
| `AY-322701` | Analytical Transmitter | Process stream gas analyzer, e.g., NH3/CO2 ratio or tail-gas oxygen/hydrogen content |
| `LT-322504-3` | Level Transmitter | Startup separator level monitoring transmitter |
| `HIC-329601` | Hand Indicator Controller | Auxiliary startup vent/bypass hand controller |
| `PT-323201`, `PT-329251` | Pressure Transmitter | Auxiliary separator or low-pressure steam drum pressure transmitters |
